369ab475db49\\\" class=\\\"news-post-header-image\\\" src=\\\"https://cdn4.orgsync.com/images/os-attachments/291a26c3-42f9-4bdd-b62d-369ab475db49.png?w=710\\\" style=\\\"border:none; display:block; style=\\\"\\\"><\\/td>\\r\\n<\\/tr>\\r\\n<\\/tbody>\\r\\n<\\/table>\\r\\n<br>\\r\\n<h2 align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"clear:both; color:#2b2b2b!important; font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:1.8rem; font-weight:400; line-height:120%!important; margin-bottom:.5rem; margin-top:.2rem\\\">\\r\\n[NUSSU EXCO] Termination of Grabwheels Services on Campus <\\/h2>\\r\\n<br>\\r\\n<div class=\\\"ck-content-only\\\">\\r\\n<ol style=\\\"font-family:inherit; font-size:1rem; line-height:1.6; list-style:outside; margin:0 0 1.33333rem 1.4rem; padding:0\\\">\\r\\n<li style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<span style=\\\"font-size:16px\\\">We refer to the press release by Land Transport Authority (LTA) on 4 November 2019 titled \\u201c<strong>E-Scooters to Be Prohibited on All Footpaths Following Safety Review\\u201d<\\/strong>. The new regulation will be implemented from today,\\r\\n 5 November 2019.<\\/span><\\/p>\\r\\n<\\/li><li value=\\\"2\\\" style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<span style=\\\"font-size:16px\\\">As NUS does not have the necessary infrastructure, GrabWheels has terminated its service across the university in compliance with the above regulation. This has been in effect since 2359 hrs yesterday, 4 November 2019.&nbsp;<\\/span><\\/p>\\r\\n<\\/li><li value=\\\"3\\\" style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<span style=\\\"font-size:16px\\\">NUSSU EXCO has been working closely with University Campus Infrastructure (UCI) and GrabWheels. We will continue to monitor and collaborate on the progressive removal of GrabWheels parking stations, e-scooters and collateral across\\r\\n the university.<\\/span><\\/p>\\r\\n<\\/li><li value=\\\"4\\\" style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<span style=\\\"font-size:16px\\\">NUSSU EXCO recognises the continued efforts by the LTA in ensuring the safe usage of motorised Personal Mobility Devices (PMDs). The decision to ban them was attributed to errant behaviour by motorists and an increasing number of\\r\\n e-scooter related incidents.<\\/span><\\/p>\\r\\n<\\/li><li value=\\\"5\\\" style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<span style=\\\"font-size:16px\\\">The safety and well-being of NUS students is of our utmost priority. We recognise that since the implementation of GrabWheels across the university, there have been several safety-related accidents.<\\/span><\\/p>\\r\\n<\\/li><li value=\\\"6\\\" style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<span style=\\\"font-size:16px\\\">NUSSU EXCO is open to green mobility options across the university.&nbsp;However, it is important that these options are effectively integrated with our campus infrastructure. NUSSU EXCO will continue to advocate for the development\\r\\n of such infrastructure that will be capable of accommodating future&nbsp;initiatives.<\\/span><\\/p>\\r\\n<\\/li><li value=\\\"7\\\" style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<span style=\\\"font-size:16px\\\">While this change might inconvenience some, we hope that students will feel safer commuting around campus. NUSSU EXCO calls for the relevant NUS offices to continue working with us through consistent cooperation and dialogue.<\\/span><\\/p>\\r\\n<\\/li><li value=\\\"8\\\" style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<span style=\\\"font-size:16px\\\">If you require any assistance or clarifications, please feel free to contact us at\\r\\n<strong>feedback@nussu.org.sg<\\/strong>.<\\/span><\\/p>\\r\\n<\\/li><\\/ol>\\r\\n<\\/div>\\r\\n<center><br>\\r\\n<table class=\\\"email-ready-button \\\" bgcolor=\\\"#82a941\\\" style=\\\"border-radius:4px; Most accept their place in a system favouring the strong. Others\\r\\n have sought to protect themselves through alliances or by making themselves indispensable through developing niche capabilities or adopting activist foreign policies. Zhou Xizhuang Michael, Council Chairperson, presided at this second scheduled\\r\\n meeting. The following were the agenda tabled for and discussed at the meeting:<\\/p>\\r\\n<ol style=\\\"font-family:inherit; font-size:1rem; line-height:1.6; list-style:lower-alpha outside; margin:0 0 1.33333rem 1.4rem; padding:0\\\">\\r\\n<li style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">Approval of the Allocation of Subscription Fees<\\/li><li style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">Endorsement of the Union Budget<\\/li><li style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">Appointment and Election of the Finance Standing Committee Members<\\/li><li style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">Appointment and Election of the Union Adjudication Committee Members<\\/li><li style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\">Discussion of Senior Management Dialogue Agenda<\\/li><\\/ol>\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<strong>2.<\\/strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The allocation of subscription fees was proposed to the Council by the Executive Committee. A formal vote took place, and the vote passed unanimously by the Council.<\\/p>\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<strong>3.<\\/strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The Union budget consists of the budget of the Executive Committee and the budgets of the fifteen Constituent Bodies. Following the presentation of and the Council\\u2019s approval for the budgets of the Executive Committee and all the\\r\\n Constituent Bodies, the Council endorsed the Union Budget unanimously.<\\/p>\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<strong>4.<\\/strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The Council appointed the Finance Standing Committee. Three Council Representatives were nominated and elected by the Council as members of the committee. The following is the list of committee members of the Finance Standing Committee:<\\/p>\\r\\n<ol style=\\\"font-family:inherit; font-size:1rem; line-height:1.6; list-style:lower-alpha outside; margin:0 0 1.33333rem 1.4rem; padding:0\\\">\\r\\n<li style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\"><strong>Andrik Kok Zi Shen<\\/strong> (FASS Club Exco Representative/ Financial Secretary),\\r\\n<strong><em>ex officio<\\/em> Chairman<\\/strong>;<\\/li><li style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\"><strong>Wang Kai Richard<\\/strong> (FASS Club Exco Representative/ Union President),\\r\\n<strong><em>ex officio<\\/em> Member<\\/strong>;<\\/li><li style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\"><strong>Muhammad Quraishi<\\/strong> (NUSPA President/ Council Representative ),\\r\\n<strong>Member<\\/strong>;<\\/li><li style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\"><strong>Chuan Jun Kai<\\/strong> (Science Club President/ Council Representative),\\r\\n<strong>Member<\\/strong>;<\\/li><li style=\\\"font-weight:300\\\"><strong>Tay Wei David<\\/strong> (Science Club Exco Representative/ Human Resource Director),\\r\\n<strong>Member<\\/strong>.<\\/li><\\/ol>\\r\\n<p align=\\\"left\\\" style=\\\"font-family:helvetica,arial,verdana,sans-serif; font-size:15px; font-weight:300; line-height:22px; margin:1em 0 19px\\\">\\r\\n<strong>5.<\\/strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The Council appointed the Union Adjudication Committee.
